## Page 4

<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">随着互联网和数字化技术的飞速发展，大数据成为热门的技术领域。特别是</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">2019</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 年国家</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">明确将“数据”视为生产要素以来，大数据技术的发展更加迅猛，已经成为现代社会各行各</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">业发展的“最大变量”。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">掌握大数据技术，对于程序员来说，可以极大地提升职场价值和社会价值。然而，作者</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">在学习</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">MapReduce</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Spark</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 的时候，有多次从入门到放弃的经历。相关的技术教程很多，即</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">使按照教程一步步学习，也往往不得其解，过了一段时间就忘掉了，需要从头再学。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">现有的大数据技术非常多，如</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Hive</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">MPP</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Spark</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Flink</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Kafka</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Hudi</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Iceberg</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 等，这</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">些技术往往很复杂，学习代价也很大。即使下定决心去学一种技术，也会因为不知道这种技</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">术对未来工作有没有用，而带着质疑去学习，效果可想而知。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">如果有这么一本书，像讲故事一样，描述用特定大数据技术解决一些业务问题的项目经</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">历，在各种大数据使用场景中引领读者学习各种大数据技术的具体应用，那么读者就可以参</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">照这些场景，并结合自己的实际工作，从应用出发，带着一些具体问题，研究对应的大数据</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">技术，这样的学习是更有效的。这就是本书的意义所在。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">下面对本书的结构脉络进行说明。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#00aeef">1.</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#00aeef"> 大数据技术应用场景选取</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">本书以大数据技术应用场景进行章节划分，所述场景力求全面，而金融业在大数据技术</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">运用的深度和广度上都有优势，且应用场景比较典型。在过去的十几年里，作者团队一直扎</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">根金融大数据技术研发，对大数据技术体系的庞大和应用场景的复杂多样深有体会，且积累</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">了大量实战经验。本书由团队中不同大数据领域的十几位技术负责人编写，囊括丰富的大数</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">据应用场景，涉及常用的大数据技术。本书将这些场景分成五类。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">1</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">数据处理类：将数据从业务系统采集到数据仓库，以及在数据仓库做批量加工或者流</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">式加工。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">2</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">数据使用类：数据加工完成以后，以数据服务、数据可视化图表的方式给到业务系</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">统，并满足数据使用过程中的响应速度要求。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">数据治理类：大数据所有端到端过程中的质量管理、元数据管理、安全管理。</span>

<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">.</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:7.76pt;color:#000000">Ⅲ</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:7.76pt;color:#000000"> </span>

![](./从程序员到架构师：大数据技术金融级全场景应用实战_王伟杰，赵世辉_15619042_9787111774945_assets/images/p004_img01.png)

前言

---

## Page 5

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef">从程序员到架构师</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef">：</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef">大数据技术金融级全场景应用实战</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">4</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">数据运维类：大数据系统中的作业调度、跨环境部署、计算资源管理。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">5</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">综合场景类：一些特殊的综合场景，如数据湖、流批一体、信创等。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">除了在本集团落地以外，团队解决大数据应用问题的方案或产品也会输出到同行业其他</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">公司和其他行业的公司。在与同行的交流当中，作者发现，虽然团队使用的有些技术架构不</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">是最前沿的（因为金融业比较注重稳定性和安全性），但是几乎覆盖大数据能碰到的所有场</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">景，所以本书所选的场景，应该可以满足大部分大数据技术人员的诉求。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#00aeef">2.</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#00aeef"> 每个场景的编写脉络</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">本书每个场景基本都是按照如下脉络展开的。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">1</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">描述业务需求。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">2</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">分析业务需求对应要解决的技术问题，归纳出几个待解决的技术难点。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">阐述每个技术难点的解决思路。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">4</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">针对解决思路进行技术选型。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">5</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">分析针对每一个难点的解决方案。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">6</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">整合得到整体解决方案和技术架构。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">7</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">阐述方案落地时的技术要点或注意事项。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">8</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">介绍方案实际应用效果。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">9</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">分析架构的优缺点、使用注意事项、不适合的场景（使用限制）。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">以上内容基本是按照大数据架构师碰到特定业务问题时，从需求分析到方案落地，再到</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">事后总结的整个历程编排的。读者阅读时，可以从架构师的角度进行思考，也能够习得架构</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">师的一些实战经验。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">本书基于场景进行大数据技术应用讲解，在以下几个方面可以帮助读者。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#00aeef">1.</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#00aeef"> 学习新技术</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">开发人员学习新技术时，可能已经确定这项技术要用在哪里，比如，为了快速搜索一个</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">有上千万条记录的大表，就去学习</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Elasticsearch</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">；也可能并不清楚这项技术的用途，比如，因</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">为很流行用</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Spark</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000"> 作为大数据平台，所以就去学习。这两种情况里，前者往往通过相关教程</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">或者官方文档就能上手使用，但是对于后者，开发人员在学习过程中可能经常会想，为什</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">么要有某个功能？为什么会有</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">Shuffle</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">？结果资料看完了，对技术如何使用还是云里雾</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">里的。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">阅读这本书，在应用场景中学技术，知道某项技术能解决什么问题，也就能理解它为什</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">么那样设计，才能真正学会它。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#00aeef">2.</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#00aeef"> 发挥数据的业务价值</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">技术人员都希望利用自己的技术能力提供业务价值，在大数据平台中，就是利用大数据</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">技术挖掘数据的价值。但是实现这个目标并不容易，需要丰富的实战经验，对于新手来说，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">往往要花费不少时间进行诸多项目的历练。这时就可以参考本书，对照自己的任务需求找到</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">类似的项目实施过程。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:7.76pt;color:#000000">Ⅳ</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:7.76pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">.</span>

![](./从程序员到架构师：大数据技术金融级全场景应用实战_王伟杰，赵世辉_15619042_9787111774945_assets/images/p005_img01.png)

## Page 6

<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#00aeef">3.</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#00aeef"> 提升自我价值</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">如果想成为一名架构师，需要在哪些方面有所提升？需要做些什么？答案可能是，列</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">出几个甚至几十个维度，对照自己的不足逐个进行改进。作者认为，有一个更简单的答案：</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">某个项目需要设计方案去实现某种相对较新的功能，如果能够给出可行方案，那就是完成了</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">一项架构师工作。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">对于一个新的项目需求，可以通过自己之前的项目经历去解决，本书的案例也能提供一</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">些参考。希望本书能够帮助技术人员为公司解决更多的实际问题，提升自我价值。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#00aeef">4.</span><span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#00aeef"> 面试展示</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">面试的时候，通常面试官会了解一下候选人的具体项目或架构经历，很多候选人无法清</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">楚展现自己解决问题的过程和其间发挥的作用。本书提供了大量的实战案例，并且每个案例</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">都非常详细地阐述了从业务需求到技术落地过程中方方面面的考量，能为读者的项目经历展</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">示提供一些参考，阅读中的思考过程也能帮助读者对大数据技术应用和项目实施进行梳理与</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">总结。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">需要注意的是，本书基于实战经历编写，注重业务需求描述和技术应用讲解，目的是让</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">读者深入业务去理解技术，如果想具体学习某一项技术的使用方法，可以阅读相应的图书、</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">官方文档等资料。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">相信读者在了解以上编写思路后，在阅读本书时会更有针对性。接下来，请开启基于全</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSYK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#000000">场景应用实战学习大数据技术的历程吧。</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef">前</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef"> </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef">言</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#00aeef">编</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:10.29pt;color:#00aeef"> </span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.29pt;color:#00aeef">者</span>

<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">.</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:7.76pt;color:#000000">Ⅴ</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:7.76pt;color:#000000"> </span>

![](./从程序员到架构师：大数据技术金融级全场景应用实战_王伟杰，赵世辉_15619042_9787111774945_assets/images/p006_img01.png)

## Page 7

<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">  16. 4. 1 </span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">重</span><span style="font-family:'E-B6';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">技术</span><span style="font-family:'E-B6';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 不重</span><span style="font-family:'E-B6';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">业务</span><span style="font-family:'E-B6';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">  </span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">/  250</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">  16. 4. 2 </span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">重</span><span style="font-family:'E-B6';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">继承</span><span style="font-family:'E-B6';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 不重</span><span style="font-family:'E-B6';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">创新</span><span style="font-family:'E-B6';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">  </span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">/  250</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">  16. 4. 3 </span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">重</span><span style="font-family:'E-B6';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">功能</span><span style="font-family:'E-B6';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 不重</span><span style="font-family:'E-B6';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">非功能</span><span style="font-family:'E-B6';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">  </span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">/  250</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">  16. 4. 4 </span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">技术上重</span><span style="font-family:'E-B6';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">深度</span><span style="font-family:'E-B6';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 不重</span><span style="font-family:'E-B6';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">广度</span><span style="font-family:'E-B6';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">  </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef">目</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef"> </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef">录</span>

## Page 18

<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">为了帮助读者更好地理解本书中的金融行业大数据技术场景</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">有必要对金融大数据技术发展</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">历程以及主要技术栈做一个简要介绍</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">通过学习</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">读者能够更好把握金融大数据技术演进脉络</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">深入地体会当前主流大数据平台各类技术的成因</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">并结合在本书提供的各个场景实战中锻炼而成</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">的能力</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">形成符合自身实际情况的大数据平台方案</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">更加有效地满足实际业务需求</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Avanti';font-size:13.68pt;color:#ffffff">1</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:13.68pt;color:#ffffff">.</span><span style="font-family:'Avanti';font-size:13.68pt;color:#ffffff"> 1</span><span style="font-family:'FZZHUNYSK--GBK1-0';font-size:13.68pt;color:#00aeef"> 金融大数据技术发展历程</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">金融大数据处理技术是随着信息化的不断推进而逐渐发展成熟的</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">从</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">20</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 世纪</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">80</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 年代开始</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">金融业的后台业务处理开始电子化</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">到了</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">20</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 世纪</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">90</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 年代初期</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">我国颁布的</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">《</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">国务院关于金融体</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">制改革的决定</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">》</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">中指出</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">：“</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">加快金融电子化建设</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">推广计算机的运用和开发</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">实现联行清算</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">信</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">贷储蓄</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">信息统计</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">业务处理和办公的自动化</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">”，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">之后产生了越来越多的电子化处理系统</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">但是</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">由于当时的系统没有联网</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">数据无法统一规划</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">同一份数据需要在多个系统中重复录入</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">重复保</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">存</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">各系统的数据定义</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">采集流程也自成体系</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">相同业务含义的数据在不同系统中取值不同</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">无</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">法简单</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">快速地汇集</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">因此</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">直到</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">2000</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 年前后</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">随着网络技术的快速发展和应用</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">才出现了真正</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">意义上的数据处理技术</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">图</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">1-1</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 展示了</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">2000</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 年以来金融大数据技术的发展路径</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>

<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef">·</span><span style="font-family:'FZFSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef">图</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef">1-1</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'FZFSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">金融大数据技术发展路径</span>

<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef">1.</span><span style="font-family:'FZS3JW--GB1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef"> 数据仓库</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">2000</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 年前后</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">网络技术的发展把金融业的单机版系统升级为城市综合网</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">实现了同城</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">同</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">省</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">全国的通存通兑</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">信息化技术的运用也从原来的储蓄</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">会计等柜面业务和后台核算业务扩展</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">到信贷统计</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">资金调拨业务领域</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">并逐步发展到了办公自动化</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">决策支持等银行业务和管理的方</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:7.76pt;color:#000000">2 </span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">.</span>

![](./从程序员到架构师：大数据技术金融级全场景应用实战_王伟杰，赵世辉_15619042_9787111774945_assets/images/p018_img01.jpg)

![](./从程序员到架构师：大数据技术金融级全场景应用实战_王伟杰，赵世辉_15619042_9787111774945_assets/images/p018_img02.png)

1数据仓库  2.数据仓库+数据湖  3云原生大数据平台
·商业产品  ·开放体系的商业产品  ·多元化的开源技术
·结构化数据  ·结构化+非结构化数据  ·多模态数据的融合
·整合报表等应用  ·自主用数分析  ·数据的智能应用

## Page 19

<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">方面面</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">实现了全系统的电子化和网络化</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">随着系统的增多</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">跨系统的数据交换和整合成为数据</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">处理的主要任务</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">金融业开始建立专用的数据处理系统</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">通过一系列标准和规范来解决数据整合</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">的问题</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">当时大型金融机构采用的主流数据处理产品是</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Oracle Exadata</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Teradata</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 等</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">处理的数据</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">量在</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">TB</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 级</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">主要场景是完成跨部门</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">跨业务</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">跨时间</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">跨平台的数据仓库应用</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">支持各类数据的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">分发和管理类报表</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">如监管报表</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">）。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef">2.</span><span style="font-family:'FZS3JW--GB1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef"> 数据仓库</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef">+</span><span style="font-family:'FZS3JW--GB1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef">数据湖</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">到了</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">2010</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 年前后</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">随着分布式和并行数据处理技术的发展成熟</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">海量大数据处理技术开始走</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">向</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">平民化</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">”，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">即使普通的</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">x86</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 设备</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">也可以搭建类似</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Teradata</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 的大规模并行处理系统</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">其中的典</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">型技术包括</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Greenplum</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Hadoop</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> （</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">如国外商业版本的</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">CDH</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">HDP</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">以及华为</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">FusionInsight HD</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 等</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">）。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">从此大数据处理不再依靠昂贵</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">封闭的设备</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">存储和加工成本的降低使数据量快速增长</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">金融业</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">进入真正的</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">大数据时代</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">”。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">随着数据量的急剧增长以及非结构化数据</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">如图片</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">视频</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">语音等</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">的运用</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">传统数据仓库</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">技术已经无法满足数据处理需求</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">数据湖技术应运而生</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">数据湖最初由存储厂商提出</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">其目的是</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">满足企业以较低成本存储数据的要求</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">随着数据湖技术的发展</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">支持的大数据场景越来越多</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">特</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">别是数据湖提出的</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">数据驱动</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 理念</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">改变了数据仓库</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">应用驱动</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 的模式</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">使数据湖成为金融</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">场景创新的主要技术</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">其低廉的建设成本也使之成为中小型金融企业大数据平台的主流技术</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">这</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">个时期</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">大数据承载的业务场景已经从原来的固定分析报表转向自主分析挖掘</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">一方面借助数据</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">仓库的整合数据</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">可以对各类数据进行多维度的灵活分析</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">；</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">另一方面</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">数据科学家能够借助数据</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">湖丰富的原始数据进行自由探索和创新</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">将大数据分析提升到了新的阶段</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">对于很多大中型金融机构来说</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">数据仓库发展历史较长</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">积累了绝大部分高价值密度的数据</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">是大数据加工分析的主要环境</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">数据湖作为补充</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">更多承载的是创新性业务</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">所以这两条技术路</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">线并行发展</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">并没有深度融合或相互替代</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef">3.</span><span style="font-family:'FZS3JW--GB1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef"> 云原生大数据平台</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">到了</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">2020</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 年前后</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">云原生</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Cloud-Native</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">技术的广泛应用加速了大数据技术的发展</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">云原</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">生提供的存储与网络资源的灵活调度能力</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">使资源隔离和管理更加灵活高效</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">大数据技术组件可</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">以高效利用底层基础设施</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">适应更加复杂的工作负载需求</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">此外</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">云原生技术的标准化特点也使</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">更多数据种类</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">结构化和非结构化</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">和更多处理方式</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">批量和流式</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">的数据分析融合成为可能</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">实现更加复杂化</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">智能化的应用</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">这个时期</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">云计算技术也得到了飞速发展</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">该技术提供了存储</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">计算分离和资源的动态伸缩能力</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">这对大数据技术至关重要</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">既满足了大数据应用多样化的部署</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">需求</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">又可以降低大规模资源下的总体拥有成本</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">此外</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">这个阶段影响大数据技术发展的另一个</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">因素是开源技术</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">一方面</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">开源技术为大数据提供了多样化的技术</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">满足了特色化的数据处理场</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">景</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">；</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">另一方面</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">突破了很多的技术限制</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">如</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">MPP</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 数据库技术限制</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">），</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">解决了原有应用在时效性</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">访问效率等方面的难题</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">云原生技术也让大数据开发和处理过程变得更加复杂</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">想要每一位开发或分析人员都掌握如</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">此多的技术几乎是不可能的</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">必须借助体系化的大数据平台</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">以</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">PaaS</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 化的理念将这些技术进行有</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef">第</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef">1</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef"> 章</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.73pt;color:#333333">金融大数据应用概述</span>

<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">.</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:7.76pt;color:#000000">3 </span>

![](./从程序员到架构师：大数据技术金融级全场景应用实战_王伟杰，赵世辉_15619042_9787111774945_assets/images/p019_img01.png)

## Page 20

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef">从程序员到架构师</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef">：</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef">大数据技术金融级全场景应用实战</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">机集成</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">从而提升大数据的开发和处理效率</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">那么</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">市面上可用的大数据技术有哪些</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">？</span>
<span style="font-family:'Avanti';font-size:13.68pt;color:#ffffff">1</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:13.68pt;color:#ffffff">.</span><span style="font-family:'Avanti';font-size:13.68pt;color:#ffffff"> 2</span><span style="font-family:'FZZHUNYSK--GBK1-0';font-size:13.68pt;color:#00aeef"> 大数据技术分类</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">从大数据技术发展历程可以看出</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">无论在</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">哪个阶段</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">大数据技术都是围绕如何承载数据</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">挖掘数据价值发展的</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">虽然技术多样</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">但核心</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">技术主要包括数据采集</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">数据存储</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">数据加工</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">和数据分析四大类</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">如图</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">1-2</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 所示</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef">1.</span><span style="font-family:'FZS3JW--GB1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef"> 数据采集</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">数据采集是数据处理的起点</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">用于获取有用的信息</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">是大数据发展的关键技术</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">数据采集需</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">要从各种源头获取结构化</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">半结构化或非结构化的数据</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">这些数据来自交易系统</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">用户行为等多</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">元化渠道</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">数据也有批量</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">流式等多种形式</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">以上因素交织在一起</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">使数据采集技术变得非常复</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">杂</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">包括数据接口采集</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">行为数据埋点采集</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">物联网数据采集</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">网络爬虫采集等</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">开源的数据采</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">集技术有很多</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">如</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Apache Flume</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Logstash</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Fluentd</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Apache Chukwa</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Scrapy</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Elastic Beats</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Apache Flink CDC</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 等</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef">2.</span><span style="font-family:'FZS3JW--GB1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef"> 数据存储</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">数据采集之后</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">就要进行有效且持久的存储</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">以备数据分析和应用</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">面对不同规模</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">类型的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">数据</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">选择合适的存储技术是确保数据安全</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">可靠和高效访问的关键</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">金融业涉及的数据类型繁</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">多</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">数据量庞大</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">并且要满足高可用性</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">高并发性和低延迟等要求</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">单一的存储技术很难应对</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">所以</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">一般会采用多种存储技术来共同完成</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">最为常见的是数据库和分布式文件系统相结合的模</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">式</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">：</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">数据库用于存储结构化数据</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">提供高效的事务处理和复杂查询功能</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">；</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">分布式文件系统则用于</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">存储非结构化数据</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">提供高吞吐量和可扩展的存储能力</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">在大数据使用的关系数据库中</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">基于</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">MPP</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 架构的有</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Greenplum</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Vertica</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Apache Doris</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Citus</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">等</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">基于</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Hadoop</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 的有</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Apache Hive</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Apache HBase</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Apache Cassandra</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 等</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">它们在不同的场景和需</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">求下提供了不同的功能与特性</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">对于分布式文件系统</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">目前比较流行的有</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">HDFS</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 和对象存储</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">HDFS</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 本身就是一项开源技术</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">开源的对象存储方案有</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Ceph</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">MinIO</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">OpenIO</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 等</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef">3.</span><span style="font-family:'FZS3JW--GB1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef"> 数据加工</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">数据加工的本质在于整合和转化数据资源</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">使之从原始</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">零散的状态转化为有价值的洞察与</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">决策依据</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">如同石油</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">未被提炼之前仅仅是埋藏在地下的自然资源</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">价值并未得到充分体现</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">一</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">旦经过精炼加工</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">不仅能成为汽车</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">飞机的主要燃料</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">还可以被加工成塑料</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">化妆品等高附加值</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">产品</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">同样</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">大数据作为信息时代的</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">石油</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">”，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">也需要经过处理和加工才能从中提取有价值的信</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">息</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">数据经过清洗和预处理</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">去除错误或不完整的数据</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">将看似杂乱无章的数据转化为有价值的</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:7.76pt;color:#000000">4 </span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">.</span>

<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef"> ·</span><span style="font-family:'FZFSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef">图</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef">1-2</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'FZFSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">大数据技术分类</span>
