数据  数据  数据  数据
采集  存储  加工  分析

---

## Page 21

<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">信息资产</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">通过加工整合数据</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">可以获得更全面的数据视图</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">更好地理解数据的本质和规律</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">数</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">据加工可以利用</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Hadoop</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 的计算框架</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">：</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">MapReduce</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Spark</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Apache Tez</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 等</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">也可以利用数据库提供</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">的计算能力直接对数据库里面的数据进行加工</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">如果是实时加工</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">则可以使用的开源技术有</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Apache Flink</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Apache Kafka</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Apache Spark Streaming</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Apache Storm</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Apache Samza</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 等</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef">4.</span><span style="font-family:'FZS3JW--GB1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef"> 数据分析</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">想要从海量数据中挖掘有价值的信息</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">需要数据分析技术作为支撑</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">传统的数据分析技术受</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">计算能力和分析方法的限制</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">难以应对</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">PB</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 级数据量及多样化数据类型</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">并且</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">在分析速度上</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">往往也无法满足实时分析的要求</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">所以数据分析技术中需要使用分布式计算实现对大规模数据的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">有效管理和高效处理</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">此外</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">在支持多样化数据分析方面</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">大数据分析技术需要具备强大的数据</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">解析能力和灵活的数据模型支持</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">以便整合各类异构数据资源</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">从中发现深层次关系及模式</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">数据分析最常用到的是</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">OLAP</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> （</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">On-Line Analytical Processing</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">联机分析处理</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">），</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">主流的</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">OLAP</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">引擎有基于</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">MPP</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 架构的</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">ClickHouse</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Apache Presto</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Apache Impala</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Apache Doris</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 等</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">基于预计算</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">的</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Apache Druid</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Apache Kylin</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 等</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">基于搜索引擎架构的</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Elasticsearch</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">Apache Solr</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 等</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">但是数据分析不能等同于</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">OLAP</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">因为数据分析还有包含数据挖掘</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">可视化报表等领域的场</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">景</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">这些领域本身也是非常复杂的领域</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">本节就不再展开了</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">本节举例的大数据技术</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">只是市面上开源技术的一小部分</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">还有大量的商业技术和开源技术</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">没有包括其中</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">并且</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">一些大数据的应用</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">并不是单纯使用大数据技术就可以完成的</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">在后续的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">场景实战中</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">还需要用到一些微服务</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">容器等技术</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">这些通常也不会归纳为大数据技术</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">本节简单介绍了大数据技术的分类</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">接下来介绍一下本书要覆盖的应用场景</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Avanti';font-size:13.68pt;color:#ffffff">1</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:13.68pt;color:#ffffff">.</span><span style="font-family:'Avanti';font-size:13.68pt;color:#ffffff"> 3</span><span style="font-family:'FZZHUNYSK--GBK1-0';font-size:13.68pt;color:#00aeef"> 金融大数据技术应用场景</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">本书共介绍了十几个应用场景</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">这些场景并未按照数据采集</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">存储</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">加工</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">分析这样的技术</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">分类</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">因为很多场景可能需要使用多个技术</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">本书提供的场景基本是按照数据处理</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">数据使用</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">数据治理</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">部署运维和综合类场景这</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">5</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 个部分来展开的</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">第</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">1</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 部分为数据处理计算类场景</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">分别为数据采集</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">数据离线处理</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">流式数据处理</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">第</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">2</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 部分为数据使用类场景</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">分别为给系统使用加工完数据的数据服务和利用数据分析工具</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">的数据加速场景</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">在完成整个数据研发的链条当中</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">会涉及一些治理相关的场景</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">也就是本书的第</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 部分</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">———</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">数据治理类场景</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">本书将会介绍元数据管理</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">数据安全管理和数据质量管理</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 个场景</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">大数据程序研发完后</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">将会碰到一些部署运维类场景</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">包含大数据作业调度</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">大数据计算资</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">源管理</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">三态投产</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">这就是本书的第</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">4</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 部分</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">在完成前面四个部分的场景实战后</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">本书的第</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">5</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 部分将介绍一些综合类场景</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">包含流批一体</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">数据湖和建设自主可控的信创大数据平台</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">本书的场景分类如图</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">1-3</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 所示</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef">第</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef">1</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef"> 章</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.73pt;color:#333333">金融大数据应用概述</span>

## Page 22

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef">从程序员到架构师</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef">：</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef">大数据技术金融级全场景应用实战</span>

<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef">·</span><span style="font-family:'FZFSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef">图</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#00aeef">1-3</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'FZFSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">场景分类</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">这些场景在金融大数据领域都非常重要</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">涉及的技术也多种多样</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">通过对本书的学习</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">读者</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">不仅能对金融大数据技术和应用有更深入</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">全面的理解</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">还能建立起一套适应大数据时代的开发</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">体系和思维模式</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">同时提升在大数据领域的专业素养和技术能力</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">帮助解决实际工作中的问题</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">此外</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">通过场景案例分析和实践操作</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">能够拓宽技术和业务视野</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">培养思考和创新能力</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">在大数</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">据领域中不断提升自身竞争力</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">以应对未来职业发展中的挑战</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>

<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:7.76pt;color:#000000">6 </span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">.</span>

## Page 23

<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">在谈论数据采集时</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">读者的理解可能不一样</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">根据作者多年经验</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">有些互联网公司会用数据</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">库点对点采集数据</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">所以其采集方式是数据库间的复制</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">；</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">有些银行不允许同时访问业务系统的数</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">据库和数据仓库的数据库</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">这就要求业务系统将数据库的数据写入文件</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">再传递到数据仓库能访</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">问的文件系统</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">；</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">而有些监管系统的需求则是将多个机构上传的数据文件归拢存放在一个地方</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">所</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">以其采集系统既要有各机构上传情况的管理功能</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">又要有数据整合和加载到数据库的能力</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">本章不讨论采集的定义</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">直接用一个作者碰到的场景介绍逐步迭代改进数据采集架构的过程</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">本章有</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 个架构方案</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">逐步迭代</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">由浅入深</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Avanti';font-size:13.68pt;color:#ffffff">2</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:13.68pt;color:#ffffff">.</span><span style="font-family:'Avanti';font-size:13.68pt;color:#ffffff"> 1</span><span style="font-family:'FZZHUNYSK--GBK1-0';font-size:13.68pt;color:#00aeef"> 数据采集业务场景</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">某银行的手机</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">APP</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 中有一个理财栏目</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">用户可以在这个栏目浏览理财产品并下单购买</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">资金</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">直接从用户个人储蓄卡中扣除</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">整个业务流程分为下列</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 个步骤</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">1</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">获取理财产品列表信息</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">用户在手机银行</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">APP</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 发起理财产品查询</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">请求发送到手机银行后端系统</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">手机银行后端系统</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">调用理财系统</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">理财产品查询</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 交易码</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">获取可选的产品列表信息</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">2</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">理财产品下单购买</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">用户从产品列表中选择意向产品</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">并发起产品购买动作</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">请求经过手机银行后端系统被发送</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">到理财系统</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">理财系统调用对私存款系统的交易码</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">对用户个人储蓄卡执行资金扣除动作</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">银行卡余额扣除通知</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">在用户的个人储蓄卡账户余额扣除或者资金入账时</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">余额变动消息将以短信的形式发送给</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">用户</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">为了提升理财产品销售额以及用户体验</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">业务部门提出了以下需求</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">：</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">根据用户在理财栏目的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">浏览行为</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">购买行为</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">构建用户画像</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">当用户有资金入账时</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">在余额变动的短信尾部增加理财产</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">品推荐内容</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">用户根据推荐链接可以直接购买理财产品</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">想要实现这个需求</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">至少需要获取以下数据</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">：</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">1</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">用户在手机银行</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">APP</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 上的浏览行为数据</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">2</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">用户余额变动消息</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">用户实际下单购买的理财产品数据</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">4</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">用户过往的理财数据</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>

<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">.</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:7.76pt;color:#000000">7 </span>

## Page 24

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef">从程序员到架构师</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef">：</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.73pt;color:#00aeef">大数据技术金融级全场景应用实战</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">从技术角度来说</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">上述数据可分为如下类型</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">：</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">1</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">前端用户行为数据</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">2</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">服务端应用层数据</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">如余额变动消息</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">）。</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">）</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">数据库数据</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">以上就是业务侧的需求</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">这个需求也是变化的</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">最初</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">用户画像初始需求要求的时效是</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">T+1</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">也就是要求画像需要基于前一天的数据构建</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">一般也叫批量采集</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">）。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">之后</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">业务方希望时效可以</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">改为</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">T+0</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">而后</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">因为更多的业务应用也需要建设采集场景</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">所以需要作者所在的项目组建设一</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">个通用的采集平台</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">因此</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">本章中的方案迭代了</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 次</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">首先</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">基于</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">HDFS</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 的采集方案</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">满足</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">T+1</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 的需求</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">；</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">然后</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">通过局部的改进</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">迭代为</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">T + 0</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 的方案</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">；</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">最后</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">重新梳理了全域数据实时采集的需求</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">设计了</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">第</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 套方案</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">下面先介绍满足</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">T+1</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 需求的方案</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'Avanti';font-size:13.68pt;color:#ffffff">2</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:13.68pt;color:#ffffff">.</span><span style="font-family:'Avanti';font-size:13.68pt;color:#ffffff"> 2</span><span style="font-family:'FZZHUNYSK--GBK1-0';font-size:13.68pt;color:#00aeef"> 存储到</span><span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:13.68pt;color:#00aeef">HDFS</span><span style="font-family:'FZZHUNYSK--GBK1-0';font-size:13.68pt;color:#00aeef"> 的采集技术方案</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-HZ';font-size:11.74pt;color:#00aeef">2. 2. 1</span><span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:11.74pt;color:#00aeef"> 前端渠道用户行为数据采集</span>
<span style="font-family:'E-BZ';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">  </span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">前端渠道用户行为数据采集是对用户在网站</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">移动应用程序等多元化前端渠道上的各种行为</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">进行捕获和记录</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">这包括页面访问</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">搜索</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">点击</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">购买</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">评论等行为</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">前端数据的采集</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">一般也</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">称作数据埋点</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">也就是在前端代码当中</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">将每次用户行为的相关数据记录下来</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">并发送给服务端</span><span style="font-family:'E-B4';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">对于这种类型的数据采集</span>
